    <script>
        function docReady(fn) {
        	// see if DOM is already available
        	if (document.readyState === "complete" || document.readyState === "interactive") {
        		// call on next available tick
        		setTimeout(fn, 1);
        	} else {
        		document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", fn);
        	}
        }
        
        function manageLastMatterType() {
        	var pageLineage = ["680780","682197"];
        	var pageParentAssetId = 680780;
        	var pageAssetId = 680780;
        	var caseTypesAssetId = Number("725231");
        	//  In response to https://jira.squiz.net/browse/SUPPORT-455578
            var pageParentAssetIds = [725231, 725243, 725551, 725281, 725273];
        	var civilDisputesAssetId = Number("722728");
        	var minorCivilDisputesAssetId = Number("739734");
        	// Need to track which matter/ case type was last interacted with by the user
        	// Case Types (www.qcat.qld.gov.au/case-types): 725231
        	//if (pageLineage.includes("725231") && pageAssetId != caseTypesAssetId && pageParentAssetId == caseTypesAssetId) {
        	if (pageLineage.includes("725231") && pageAssetId != caseTypesAssetId && pageParentAssetIds.includes(pageParentAssetId)) {
        		console.log("Tracking last matter type: 680780");
        		localStorage.removeItem("lastMatterTypeId");
        		localStorage.removeItem("lastMatterTypeName");
        		localStorage.setItem("lastMatterTypeId", 680780 );
        		localStorage.setItem("lastMatterTypeName", "Queensland Civil and Administrative Tribunal");
        	}
        	// Need to display a back button on the Civil Disputes process page www.qcat.qld.gov.au/applications/civil-dispute-process: 722728
        	// allowing user to navigate back to their last matter/ case type
        	if (pageAssetId == civilDisputesAssetId || pageAssetId == minorCivilDisputesAssetId) {
        		setTimeout(function() {
        			var lastMatterTypeAssetId = localStorage.getItem("lastMatterTypeId");
        			console.log("Retrieving last matter type: " + lastMatterTypeAssetId);
        			if (!lastMatterTypeAssetId) {
        			    lastMatterTypeAssetId = caseTypesAssetId;
        			}
    				var cardComponentInnerHTML = document.querySelector('div.container > div.card-rows').getInnerHTML();
    				var cardHTML = '<div class="card ">';
    				cardHTML += '<a href="./?a=' + lastMatterTypeAssetId + '">';
    				cardHTML += '<div class="card-body">';
    				cardHTML += '<h4 class="card-title">Return to case type?</h4>';
    				cardHTML += '<p class="card-text">Find more information about your previously viewed case type</p>';
    				cardHTML += '<div class="card-cta">';
    				cardHTML += '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="30" height="30" viewBox="0 0 77 77">';
    				cardHTML += '<circle cx="38.104" cy="38.104" r="38.104" fill="#ecf4fb"></circle>';
    				cardHTML += '<path d="M33.144,23.314l15.397,15.294l-15.42,15.737" style="fill:none;stroke:#00456b;stroke-width:7px;" stroke-linecap="round"></path>';
    				cardHTML += '</svg>';
    				cardHTML += '</div>';
    				cardHTML += '</div>';
    				cardHTML += '';
    				cardHTML += '</a>';
    				cardHTML += '</div>';
    				cardComponentInnerHTML += cardHTML;
    				document.querySelector('div.container > div.card-rows').innerHTML = cardComponentInnerHTML;
        		}, 1000);
        	} else {
        		if (pageLineage.includes(civilDisputesAssetId.toString()) || pageLineage.includes(minorCivilDisputesAssetId.toString())) {
        			var lastMatterTypeAssetId = localStorage.getItem("lastMatterTypeId");
        			console.log("Retrieving last matter type: " + lastMatterTypeAssetId);
        			// references to a CTA strip which has been inserted on child pages with class of cta-back-to-matter
        			// if a matter type exists updated the href to the matter type
        			if (!!lastMatterTypeAssetId) {
        				setTimeout(function() {
        					var ctaBackToMatterButton = document.querySelector('div.smp-cta-bar.cta-back-to-matter div.smp-cta-bar__cta a');
        					ctaBackToMatterButton.href = './?a=' + lastMatterTypeAssetId;
        
        				}, 1000);
        			}
        		}
        	}
        };
        
        docReady(manageLastMatterType);
    </script>

Whether you are represented or not you can still seek&nbsp;<a href="http://www.qcat.qld.gov.au/going-to-the-tribunal/legal-advice-and-representation#Legal_advice" target="_blank" title="legal advice">legal advice</a> about your rights.</p><p>In some cases, a party is automatically able to be represented. QCAT will always agree to representation:</p><ul><li>for a child or a person with impaired capacity, or</li><li>if the matter relates to disciplinary proceedings including a review of a disciplinary decision</li><li>if the enabling Act related to the matter allows it.</li></ul><p><strong><a href="https://www.qcat.qld.gov.au/resources/legal-advice-and-representation" title="Legal advice and representation">Read more &gt;</a></strong></p></div>
